#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: adm
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS adm;

CREATE TABLE `adm` (
  `id_adm` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `id_admin` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `id_jamaah` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `id_th` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `tgl_bayar` date NOT NULL,
  `nominal` int(20) NOT NULL,
  `terbilang` varchar(60) COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  `keterangan` text COLLATE latin1_general_ci NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id_adm`),
  KEY `id_jamaah` (`id_jamaah`),
  KEY `id_admin` (`id_admin`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=2241 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 COLLATE=latin1_general_ci;
